A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. The information in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and the Exhibit attached hereto are being furnished pursuant to Item 2.02 of Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and therefore shall not be deemed filed for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

<TD VALIGN="middle"><FONT STYLE="font-size:11pt"><B>For Immediate Release</B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle" ALIGN="right"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Contact: Chris Brandon</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Director - Investor Relations</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>(734) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">323-7932</FONT></B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Announces Second Quarter 2020 Financial Results
</U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Global retail sales growth (excluding foreign currency impact) of 8.1% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">U.S. same store sales growth of 16.1% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">International same store sales growth of 1.3% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Global net store growth of 84 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Diluted EPS up 36.5% to $2.99 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>ANN ARBOR,
Michigan, July</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;16, 2020: Domino&#146;s Pizza, Inc. (NYSE: DPZ),</B> the largest pizza company in the world based on global retail sales, announced results for the second quarter. Global retail sales increased 5.7% in the second
quarter, or 8.1% excluding foreign currency impact. Global retail sales in the second quarter were positively impacted by U.S. same store sales, but were negatively impacted by temporary store closures in certain international markets. U.S. same
store sales grew 16.1% during the quarter versus the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period and were positively impacted by customer ordering behavior during the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, continuing
the positive sales momentum in the Company&#146;s U.S. stores business. The international business also posted positive same store sales results, with growth of 1.3% during the quarter. The second quarter marked the 106<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of international same store sales growth and the 37<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of U.S. same store sales growth. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company had second quarter net store growth of 84 stores, comprised of 39 net new U.S. stores and 45 net new international stores. The number of temporary
store closures in certain of the Company&#146;s international markets has declined from its peak of approximately 2,400 temporary closures. Based on information reported to the Company by its master franchisees, the Company estimates that as of
July&nbsp;8, 2020, there were fewer than 600 international stores temporarily closed. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Diluted EPS for the second quarter was $2.99, up 36.5% over the
prior year quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On July&nbsp;15, 2020, the Company&#146;s Board of Directors declared a $0.78 per share quarterly dividend for shareholders of record
as of September&nbsp;15, 2020 to be paid on September&nbsp;30, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;Our focus as a global brand and the commitment of our local operators remains
steadfast on serving our customers and our communities with a convenient, affordable and safe food and service experience,&#148; said Ritch Allison, Domino&#146;s Chief Executive Officer. &#147;I have never been more proud of our system of
franchisees, operators and corporate team members for their continued passion and innovative spirit, which was evident during the second quarter.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Second Quarter Highlights (Unaudited): </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Revenues </B>increased $108.4&nbsp;million, or 13.4%, in the second quarter of 2020. This increase was
primarily due to higher global retail sales resulting from U.S. same store sales growth and an increase in U.S. store counts during the trailing four quarters, resulting in higher supply chain, U.S. franchise and U.S. Company-owned stores revenues.
These increases in revenues were partially offset by lower international franchise revenues resulting from temporary store closures in certain of the Company&#146;s international markets due to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT>
pandemic as well as pressure from the negative impact of changes in foreign currency exchange rates. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net Income</B> increased $26.3&nbsp;million, or 28.5%, in the second quarter of 2020. This increase was
primarily driven by higher income from operations resulting from increased U.S. franchise royalty revenues as well as higher supply chain margins and a lower effective tax rate as compared to the prior year quarter driven by higher tax benefits from
equity-based compensation. The increase in net income was partially offset by lower international franchise revenues and higher net interest expense resulting from a higher average debt balance and borrowings under the Company&#146;s variable
funding notes during the second quarter. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">

represents a $0.80, or 36.5%, increase over the prior year quarter. The increase in diluted EPS was driven by higher net income, as well as lower diluted share count, primarily resulting from the Company&#146;s share repurchases during the trailing
four quarters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The table below outlines certain statistical measures utilized by the Company to analyze its performance (unaudited).

borrowings during the second quarter of 2020. Subsequent to the second quarter of 2020, the Company repaid an additional $15.0&nbsp;million under its variable funding notes, and as of July&nbsp;8, 2020, the Company had $117.0&nbsp;million of
available borrowings under its $200.0&nbsp;million variable funding notes, net of letters of credit issued of $40.0&nbsp;million and borrowings outstanding of $43.0&nbsp;million. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net cash provided by operating activities was $211.8&nbsp;million during the two fiscal quarters of 2020. The Company invested $33.7&nbsp;million in capital

was approximately $178.1&nbsp;million during the two fiscal quarters of 2020 (refer to the <I>Comments on Regulation G </I>section below for additional details). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

</TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Investment in Dash Brands Ltd. </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the second quarter of 2020, a subsidiary of the Company acquired a non-controlling interest in Dash Brands Ltd., for $40.0 million. Dash Brands Ltd. is
a privately-held company that, through its subsidiaries, serves as the Company&#146;s master franchisee in China that owns and operates Domino&#146;s Pizza stores in that market. The Company is contractually required to invest an additional $40.0
million in Dash Brands Ltd. in the first quarter of 2021, assuming certain performance conditions are satisfied. If such performance conditions are not satisfied, the Company has the option to make such investment in its discretion. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Comments on Regulation G </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to the GAAP
financial measures set forth in this press release, the Company has included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial measures within the meaning of Regulation G, including free cash flow metrics. The Company has also included
metrics such as global retail sales, global retail sales growth, global retail sales growth, excluding foreign currency impact and same store sales growth, which are commonly used statistical measures in the quick-service restaurant industry that
are important to understanding Company performance. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses &#147;<B>Global retail sales</B>&#148; to refer to total worldwide retail sales at
Company-owned and franchise stores. The Company believes global retail sales information is useful in analyzing revenues because franchisees pay royalties and advertising fees that are based on a percentage of franchise retail sales. The Company
reviews comparable industry global retail sales information to assess business trends and to track the growth of the Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> brand. In addition, supply chain revenues are directly
impacted by changes in franchise retail sales. Retail sales for franchise stores are reported to the Company by its franchisees and are not included in Company revenues. &#147;<B>Global retail sales growth</B>&#148; is calculated as the change of
U.S.&nbsp;Dollar global retail sales against the comparable period of the prior year. &#147;<B>Global retail sales growth, excluding foreign currency impact</B>&#148; is calculated as the change of international local currency global retail sales
against the comparable period of the prior year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses &#147;<B>Same store sales growth</B>,&#148; which is calculated for a given period by
including only sales from stores that had sales in the comparable weeks of both years. International same store sales growth is calculated similarly to U.S. same store sales growth. Changes in international same store sales are reported excluding
foreign currency impacts, which reflect changes in international local currency sales. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses <B>&#147;Free cash flow,&#148;</B> which is
calculated as net cash provided by operating activities, less capital expenditures, both as reported under GAAP. The Company believes that the free cash flow measure is important to investors and other interested persons, and that such persons
benefit from having a measure which communicates how much cash flow is available for working capital needs or to be used for repurchasing debt, making acquisitions, repurchasing common stock or paying dividends. </P>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Founded in 1960, Domino&#146;s Pizza is the largest pizza company in the world based on retail sales, with a significant business in both delivery and carryout
pizza. It ranks among the world&#146;s top public restaurant brands with a global enterprise of more than 17,100 stores in over 90 markets. Domino&#146;s had global retail sales of over $14.3&nbsp;billion in 2019, with over $7.0&nbsp;billion in the
U.S. and nearly $7.3&nbsp;billion internationally. In the second quarter of 2020, Domino&#146;s had global retail sales of over $3.4&nbsp;billion, with over $1.9&nbsp;billion in the U.S. and over $1.5&nbsp;billion internationally. Its system is
comprised of independent franchise owners who accounted for 98% of Domino&#146;s stores as of the end of the second quarter of 2020. Emphasis on technology innovation helped Domino&#146;s achieve more than half of all global retail sales in 2019
from digital channels, primarily online ordering and mobile applications. In the U.S., Domino&#146;s generates over 65% of sales via digital channels and has developed several innovative ordering platforms, including those developed for Google Home,
Facebook Messenger, Apple Watch, Amazon Echo and Twitter &#150; as well as Domino&#146;s Hotspots<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, an ordering platform featuring over 200,000 unique,
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-traditional</FONT> delivery locations. In June 2019, through an announced partnership with Nuro, Domino&#146;s furthered its exploration and testing of autonomous pizza delivery. In late 2019, Domino&#146;s
opened the Domino&#146;s Innovation Garage adjacent to its headquarters in Ann Arbor, Michigan to fuel continued technology and operational innovation &#150; while also launching its GPS technology, allowing customers to follow the progress of the
delivery driver from store to doorstep. In <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">mid-2020,</FONT> Domino&#146;s launched a brand new way to order contactless carryout nationwide via Domino&#146;s Carside Delivery<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">TM</SUP>, which customers can choose when placing a prepaid online order. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Order &#150; <U>dominos.com</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AnyWare Ordering &#150; <U>anyware.dominos.com</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Company Info
&#150; <U>biz.dominos.com</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Twitter &#150; <U>twitter.com/dominos</U> </P>

by the use of words such as &#147;anticipates,&#148; &#147;believes,&#148; &#147;could,&#148; &#147;should,&#148; &#147;estimates,&#148; &#147;expects,&#148; &#147;intends,&#148; &#147;may,&#148; &#147;will,&#148; &#147;plans,&#148;

information and data. While we believe these expectations and projections are based on reasonable assumptions, such forward-looking statements are inherently subject to risks, uncertainties and assumptions. Important factors that could cause actual

financial performance and our ability to pay principal and interest on our indebtedness; the effectiveness of our advertising, operations and promotional initiatives; the strength of our brand, including our ability to compete in the U.S. and

developments by us, and other food-industry competitors; the impact of new or improved technologies and alternative methods of delivery on consumer behavior; our ability to maintain good relationships with and attract new franchisees, and

exchange rates; our ability to retain or replace our executive officers and other key members of management and our ability to adequately staff our stores and supply chain centers with qualified personnel; our ability to find and/or retain suitable
